<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:echter.html>echter</a></i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">efter</i>, standing beside <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:eft.html>eft</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aft-</i>.
</p>

***eclips.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eclips.html>eclips</a> (22276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">eclipse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">eclipse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">eclīpsis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔκλειψις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ékleipsis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eclipse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐκλείπω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekleípō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I abandon, go missing, vanish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐκ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:ek.html>ek</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λείπω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leípō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I leave behind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eclips.html>eclips</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eclipsen.html>eclipsen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">eclipse</span>, the blocking of light to a celestial body by another celestial body.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verduistering.html>verduistering</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">maaneclips</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">zoneclips</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***economics.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> economics (2191)</h1><br></body> 
***economie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a> (5404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">oeconomia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οἰκονομία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oikonomía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">management of a household, administration</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οἶκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oîkos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νόμος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nómos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (surface analysis <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">eco-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nomie</i>). The first recorded sense of the word <b><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a></b>, found in a work possibly composed in 1440, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> “the management of economic affairs”, in this case, of a monastery.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>economics</li>
<li>economy</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

***ecosysteem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ecosysteem.html>ecosysteem</a> (23517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">eco-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ecology</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:systeem.html>systeem</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">system</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">systema</i>), both ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ecosysteem.html>ecosysteem</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ecosystemen.html>ecosystemen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ecosysteem.html>ecosysteempje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ecology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An ecosystem, system of an ecological community of species and its environment</li></ol>

***eddy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a> (7855)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">edēa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ed-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turning, back, reverse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ēa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ed-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ea</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A current of air or water running back, or in an opposite direction to the main current.
<ul><li><b>1922</b>, A. M. Chisholm, <i>A Thousand a Plate</i>
<dl><dd>In the bow old Dobbs fought the stream cunningly, twisting the nose into <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b> and backwaters, taking advantage when he could of set of current, and when he could not, paddling doggedly, not so powerfully, perhaps, as his partner, but with equal steadiness.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A circular current; a whirlpool.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Dryden and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>And smiling <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b> dimpled on the main.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1713</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Addison" class="extiw" title="w:Joseph Addison">Joseph Addison</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cato,_a_Tragedy" class="extiw" title="w:Cato, a Tragedy">Cato</a></cite>, published 1712, [Act 2, scene 6]:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Wheel through the air, in circling <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b> play.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms CategoryTreeTag" data-ct-mode="10" data-ct-options="{quot;modequot;:10,quot;hideprefixquot;:20,quot;showcountquot;:false,quot;namespacesquot;:[0],quot;notranslationsquot;:false}"><div class="CategoryTreeSection"><div class="CategoryTreeItem"><span class="CategoryTreeBullet"><span class="CategoryTreeToggle" data-ct-title="English_words_prefixed_with_ed-" data-ct-state="collapsed">►</span> </span> English <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> prefixed with ed-</div><div class="CategoryTreeChildren" style="display:none"></div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">eddying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">eddied</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form an <a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a>; to move in, or as if in, an <a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a>; to move in a circle.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Wordsworth and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><b>Eddying</b> round and round they sink.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sinclair_Lewis" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sinclair Lewis">Sinclair <a href = vnd.unilang:lewis.html>Lewis</a></a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/en:Babbitt/Chapter_25" class="extiw" title="s:en:Babbitt/Chapter 25">Chapter 25</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Babbitt" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Babbitt">Babbitt</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Neither in his voiceless cabin, fragrant with planks of new-cut pine, nor along the lake, nor in the sunset <a href = vnd.unilang:clouds.html>clouds</a> which presently <b>eddied</b> behind the lavender-misted mountains, could Babbitt find the spirit of Paul as a reassuring presence.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***eem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eem.html>eem</a> (107228)</h1><br></body> 
***een.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> (9)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">êen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ein</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*óynos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></strong> (<i>contracted form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">'n</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Placed before a singular noun, indicating a general case of a person or thing:</span> a, an. Compare with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>one</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aaneen.html>aaneen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bijeen.html>bijeen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenmaal.html>eenmaal</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenzaam.html>eenzaam</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:enig.html>enig</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iedereen.html>iedereen</a></span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>When it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear from the context whether <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the number or the indefinite article, the former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written with acute accents: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">één</i>. In all other <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written without. For example, <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 'one of those'. But <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i> can mean both 'one apple' and 'an apple', so if the former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> intended one would write <i><b>één</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i>.</li></ul>
<dl><dt>Examples</dt></dl>
<ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a></i>: a hat; <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a></i>; an ear.</li>
<li><i><b>Eén</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>allen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>allen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <b>één</b></i>: one for all, all for one. (The <a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Three_Musketeers" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Three Musketeers">The Three Musketeers</a>.)</li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eend.html>eend</a> (5145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ent.html>ent</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eent</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ened</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*anadz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂énh₂t-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:enten.html>Ente</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ennet</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">ennet</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eender.html>eender</a> (6009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>(the) same, alike, equal
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eender.html>eender</a></b></i>  |  that's all the same to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a></dd>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eender.html>eender</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>no matter, regardless of, anyway, anyhow
<dl><dd><i>Help <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eender.html>eender</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:welke.html>welke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:manier.html>manier</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>Help each other, <b>no matter</b> where or how.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***eenheid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a> (2379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eenheit</i>, likely calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ūnitās</i>. Some modern senses likely derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Einheit</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>, analogous to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">oneness</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenheden.html>eenheden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unity</li>
<li>unit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">measure</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law enforcement</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">squad or party; member of a military organisation or law enforcement organisation; division</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> loneliness
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenzaamheid.html>eenzaamheid</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***eerder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a> (494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Reformed by epenthesis of <i>-d-</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eerre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ēriro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*airizô</i>, an adjective formed from the comparative adverb <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*airiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>earlier, former
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerdere</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:stijl.html>stijl</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leuker.html>leuker</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His <b>former</b> style <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> funnier.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vroeger.html>vroeger</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>previous, prior
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerdere</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorstellen.html>voorstellen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ambitieuzer.html>ambitieuzer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His <b>initial</b> proposals <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> more ambitious.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>earlier
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>Zoals</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezegd.html>gezegd</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">As <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <b>earlier</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vroeger.html>vroeger</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daarstraks.html>daarstraks</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>before, previously
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>Gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>niemand</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweest.html>geweest</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">To go where no one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <b>before</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>more, rather
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:struik.html>struik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That's <b>more</b> a bush than a tree.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eetkamer.html>eetkamer</a> (9863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>Dining room.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used only for relatively small dining <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a> in a family house. A dining room in a <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a> or a mansion <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called "eetzaal".
</p>

***eeuw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a> (2350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">êwe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēwa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂eyu-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vital force</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eeuwen.html>eeuwen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuwtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>century, 100 years</li>
<li>many years</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a very long time, far too long, (an) eternity</li></ol>

***eeuwig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eeuwig.html>eeuwig</a> (1529)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">êwich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēwig</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ewig</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>eternal</li></ol>
